<s> swifter far than summer's flight swifter far than youth's delight swifter far than happy night art thou come and gone as the earth when leaves are dead 5 as the night when sleep is sped as the heart when joy is fled i am left lone alone <\s>
<s> the swallow summer comes again the owlet night resumes her reign 10 but the wild swan youth is fain to fly with thee false as thou my heart each day desires the morrow sleep itself is turned to sorrow vainly would my winter borrow 15 sunny leaves from any bough <\s>
<s> lilies for a bridal bed roses for a matron's head violets for a maiden dead pansies let my flowers be 20 on the living grave i bear scatter them without a tear let no friend however dear waste one hope one fear for me <\s>

<s> there is a copy amongst the trelawny manuscripts 1 <\s>
<s> the serpent is shut out from paradise <\s>
<s> the wounded deer must seek the herb no more in which its heart cure lies the widowed dove must cease to haunt a bower like that from which its mate with feigned sighs 5 fled in the april hour <\s>
<s> i too must seldom seek again near happy friends a mitigated pain <\s>
<s> of hatred i am proud with scorn content indifference that once hurt me now is grown 10 itself indifferent but not to speak of love pity alone can break a spirit already more than bent <\s>
<s> the miserable one turns the mind's poison into food 15 its medicine is tears its evil good <\s>
<s> therefore if now i see you seldomer dear friends dear friend <\s>
<s> know that i only fly your looks because they stir griefs that should sleep and hopes that cannot die 20 the very comfort that they minister i scarce can bear yet i so deeply is the arrow gone should quickly perish if it were withdrawn <\s>
<s> when i return to my cold home you ask 25 why i am not as i have ever been <\s>
<s> you spoil me for the task of acting a forced part in life's dull scene of wearing on my brow the idle mask of author great or mean 30 in the world's carnival <\s>
<s> i sought peace thus and but in you i found it not <\s>
<s> full half an hour to day i tried my lot with various flowers and every one still said she loves me loves me not <\s>
<s> 35 and if this meant a vision long since fled if it meant fortune fame or peace of thought if it meant but i dread to speak what you may know too well still there was truth in the sad oracle <\s>
<s> the crane o'er seas and forests seeks her home no bird so wild but has its quiet nest when it no more would roam the sleepless billows on the ocean's breast break like a bursting heart and die in foam 45 and thus at length find rest doubtless there is a place of peace where my weak heart and all its throbs will cease <\s>
<s> i asked her yesterday if she believed that i had resolution <\s>
<s> one who had 50 would ne'er have thus relieved his heart with words but what his judgement bade would do and leave the scorner unrelieved <\s>
<s> these verses are too sad to send to you but that i know 55 happy yourself you feel another's woe <\s>

<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 1 <\s>
<s> one word is too often profaned for me to profane it one feeling too falsely disdained for thee to disdain it one hope is too like despair 5 for prudence to smother and pity from thee more dear than that from another <\s>
<s> i can give not what men call love but wilt thou accept not 10 the worship the heart lifts above and the heavens reject not the desire of the moth for the star of the night for the morrow the devotion to something afar 15 from the sphere of our sorrow <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a boscombe manuscript 1 <\s>
<s> when passion's trance is overpast if tenderness and truth could last or live whilst all wild feelings keep some mortal slumber dark and deep i should not weep i should not weep <\s>
<s> it were enough to feel to see thy soft eyes gazing tenderly and dream the rest and burn and be the secret food of fires unseen couldst thou but be as thou hast been 10 3 <\s>
<s> after the slumber of the year the woodland violets reappear all things revive in field or grove and sky and sea but two which move and form all others life and love <\s>

<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 1 <\s>
<s> the golden gates of sleep unbar where strength and beauty met together kindle their image like a star in a sea of glassy weather <\s>
<s> night with all thy stars look down 5 darkness weep thy holiest dew never smiled the inconstant moon on a pair so true <\s>
<s> let eyes not see their own delight haste swift hour and thy flight 10 oft renew <\s>
<s> fairies sprites and angels keep her <\s>
<s> holy stars permit no wrong <\s>

<s> lines written on hearing the news of the death of napoleon <\s>
<s> published with hellas 1821 what <\s>
<s> alive and so bold o earth <\s>
<s> art thou not overbold <\s>
<s> leapest thou forth as of old in the light of thy morning mirth the last of the flock of the starry fold <\s>
<s> leapest thou forth as of old <\s>
<s> are not the limbs still when the ghost is fled and canst thou move napoleon being dead <\s>
<s> is not thy quick heart cold <\s>
<s> what spark is alive on thy hearth <\s>
<s> is not his death knell knolled <\s>
<s> and livest thou still mother earth <\s>
<s> thou wert warming thy fingers old o'er the embers covered and cold of that most fiery spirit when it fled 15 what mother do you laugh now he is dead <\s>
<s> who has known me of old replied earth or who has my story told <\s>
<s> it is thou who art overbold <\s>
<s> and the lightning of scorn laughed forth 20 as she sung to my bosom i fold all my sons when their knell is knolled and so with living motion all are fed and the quick spring like weeds out of the dead <\s>
<s> still alive and still bold shouted earth 25 i grow bolder and still more bold <\s>
<s> the dead fill me ten thousandfold fuller of speed and splendour and mirth <\s>
<s> i was cloudy and sullen and cold like a frozen chaos uprolled 30 till by the spirit of the mighty dead my heart grew warm <\s>
<s> i feed on whom i fed <\s>
<s> ay alive and still bold <\s>
<s> muttered earth napoleon's fierce spirit rolled in terror and blood and gold 35 a torrent of ruin to death from his birth <\s>
<s> leave the millions who follow to mould the metal before it be cold and weave into his shame which like the dead shrouds me the hopes that from his glory fled <\s>
<s> 40 sonnet political greatness <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a transcript headed sonnet to the republic of benevento in the harvard manuscript book nor happiness nor majesty nor fame nor peace nor strength nor skill in arms or arts shepherd those herds whom tyranny makes tame verse echoes not one beating of their hearts history is but the shadow of their shame 5 art veils her glass or from the pageant starts as to oblivion their blind millions fleet staining that heaven with obscene imagery of their own likeness <\s>
<s> what are numbers knit by force or custom <\s>
<s> man who man would be 10 must rule the empire of himself in it must be supreme establishing his throne on vanquished will quelling the anarchy of hopes and fears being himself alone <\s>
<s> shelley in the keepsake 1829 1 <\s>
<s> do you not hear the aziola cry <\s>
<s> methinks she must be nigh said mary as we sate in dusk ere stars were lit or candles brought and i who thought 5 this aziola was some tedious woman asked who is aziola <\s>
<s> how elate i felt to know that it was nothing human no mockery of myself to fear or hate and mary saw my soul 10 and laughed and said disquiet yourself not tis nothing but a little downy owl <\s>
<s> many an eventide thy music i had heard by wood and stream meadow and mountain side 15 and fields and marshes wide such as nor voice nor lute nor wind nor bird the soul ever stirred unlike and far sweeter than them all <\s>
<s> from that moment i 20 loved thee and thy sad cry <\s>

<s> alive and so bold o earth <\s>
<s> art thou not overbold <\s>
<s> leapest thou forth as of old in the light of thy morning mirth the last of the flock of the starry fold <\s>
<s> leapest thou forth as of old <\s>
<s> are not the limbs still when the ghost is fled and canst thou move napoleon being dead <\s>
<s> is not thy quick heart cold <\s>
<s> what spark is alive on thy hearth <\s>
<s> is not his death knell knolled <\s>
<s> and livest thou still mother earth <\s>
<s> thou wert warming thy fingers old o'er the embers covered and cold of that most fiery spirit when it fled 15 what mother do you laugh now he is dead <\s>
<s> who has known me of old replied earth or who has my story told <\s>
<s> it is thou who art overbold <\s>
<s> and the lightning of scorn laughed forth 20 as she sung to my bosom i fold all my sons when their knell is knolled and so with living motion all are fed and the quick spring like weeds out of the dead <\s>
<s> still alive and still bold shouted earth 25 i grow bolder and still more bold <\s>
<s> the dead fill me ten thousandfold fuller of speed and splendour and mirth <\s>
<s> i was cloudy and sullen and cold like a frozen chaos uprolled 30 till by the spirit of the mighty dead my heart grew warm <\s>
<s> i feed on whom i fed <\s>
<s> ay alive and still bold <\s>
<s> muttered earth napoleon's fierce spirit rolled in terror and blood and gold 35 a torrent of ruin to death from his birth <\s>
<s> leave the millions who follow to mould the metal before it be cold and weave into his shame which like the dead shrouds me the hopes that from his glory fled <\s>
<s> 40 sonnet political greatness <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a transcript headed sonnet to the republic of benevento in the harvard manuscript book nor happiness nor majesty nor fame nor peace nor strength nor skill in arms or arts shepherd those herds whom tyranny makes tame verse echoes not one beating of their hearts history is but the shadow of their shame 5 art veils her glass or from the pageant starts as to oblivion their blind millions fleet staining that heaven with obscene imagery of their own likeness <\s>
<s> what are numbers knit by force or custom <\s>
<s> man who man would be 10 must rule the empire of himself in it must be supreme establishing his throne on vanquished will quelling the anarchy of hopes and fears being himself alone <\s>
<s> shelley in the keepsake 1829 1 <\s>
<s> do you not hear the aziola cry <\s>
<s> methinks she must be nigh said mary as we sate in dusk ere stars were lit or candles brought and i who thought 5 this aziola was some tedious woman asked who is aziola <\s>
<s> how elate i felt to know that it was nothing human no mockery of myself to fear or hate and mary saw my soul 10 and laughed and said disquiet yourself not tis nothing but a little downy owl <\s>
<s> many an eventide thy music i had heard by wood and stream meadow and mountain side 15 and fields and marshes wide such as nor voice nor lute nor wind nor bird the soul ever stirred unlike and far sweeter than them all <\s>
<s> from that moment i 20 loved thee and thy sad cry <\s>
<s> notes 4 ere stars ere the stars editions 1839 <\s>

<s> 19 them they editions 1839 <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 1 <\s>
<s> on whose last steps i climb trembling at that where i had stood before when will return the glory of your prime <\s>
<s> no more oh never more <\s>
<s> out of the day and night a joy has taken flight fresh spring and summer and winter hoar move my faint heart with grief but with delight no more oh never more <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 where it is entitled a lament <\s>
<s> three manuscript copies are extant the trelawny manuscript remembrance the harvard manuscript song and the houghton manuscript the last written by shelley on a flyleaf of a copy of adonais 1 <\s>
<s> swifter far than summer's flight swifter far than youth's delight swifter far than happy night art thou come and gone as the earth when leaves are dead 5 as the night when sleep is sped as the heart when joy is fled i am left lone alone <\s>
<s> the swallow summer comes again the owlet night resumes her reign 10 but the wild swan youth is fain to fly with thee false as thou my heart each day desires the morrow sleep itself is turned to sorrow vainly would my winter borrow 15 sunny leaves from any bough <\s>
<s> lilies for a bridal bed roses for a matron's head violets for a maiden dead pansies let my flowers be 20 on the living grave i bear scatter them without a tear let no friend however dear waste one hope one fear for me <\s>

<s> published in ascham's edition of the poems 1834 <\s>
<s> there is a copy amongst the trelawny manuscripts 1 <\s>
<s> the serpent is shut out from paradise <\s>
<s> the wounded deer must seek the herb no more in which its heart cure lies the widowed dove must cease to haunt a bower like that from which its mate with feigned sighs 5 fled in the april hour <\s>
<s> i too must seldom seek again near happy friends a mitigated pain <\s>
<s> of hatred i am proud with scorn content indifference that once hurt me now is grown 10 itself indifferent but not to speak of love pity alone can break a spirit already more than bent <\s>
<s> the miserable one turns the mind's poison into food 15 its medicine is tears its evil good <\s>
<s> therefore if now i see you seldomer dear friends dear friend <\s>
<s> know that i only fly your looks because they stir griefs that should sleep and hopes that cannot die 20 the very comfort that they minister i scarce can bear yet i so deeply is the arrow gone should quickly perish if it were withdrawn <\s>
<s> when i return to my cold home you ask 25 why i am not as i have ever been <\s>
<s> you spoil me for the task of acting a forced part in life's dull scene of wearing on my brow the idle mask of author great or mean 30 in the world's carnival <\s>
<s> i sought peace thus and but in you i found it not <\s>
<s> full half an hour to day i tried my lot with various flowers and every one still said she loves me loves me not <\s>
<s> 35 and if this meant a vision long since fled if it meant fortune fame or peace of thought if it meant but i dread to speak what you may know too well still there was truth in the sad oracle <\s>
<s> the crane o'er seas and forests seeks her home no bird so wild but has its quiet nest when it no more would roam the sleepless billows on the ocean's breast break like a bursting heart and die in foam 45 and thus at length find rest doubtless there is a place of peace where my weak heart and all its throbs will cease <\s>
<s> i asked her yesterday if she believed that i had resolution <\s>
<s> one who had 50 would ne'er have thus relieved his heart with words but what his judgement bade would do and leave the scorner unrelieved <\s>
<s> these verses are too sad to send to you but that i know 55 happy yourself you feel another's woe <\s>
<s> notes 10 indifference which once hurt me is now grown trelawny manuscript <\s>

<s> 28 in trelawny manuscript on 1834 editions 1839 43 when 1839 2nd edition whence 1834 1839 1st edition <\s>
<s> 48 will 1839 2nd edition shall 1834 1839 1st edition <\s>
<s> 53 unrelieved trelawny manuscript 1839 2nd <\s>
<s> edition unreprieved 1834 1839 1st edition <\s>
<s> 54 are were trelawny manuscript <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 1 <\s>
<s> one word is too often profaned for me to profane it one feeling too falsely disdained for thee to disdain it one hope is too like despair 5 for prudence to smother and pity from thee more dear than that from another <\s>
<s> i can give not what men call love but wilt thou accept not 10 the worship the heart lifts above and the heavens reject not the desire of the moth for the star of the night for the morrow the devotion to something afar 15 from the sphere of our sorrow <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a boscombe manuscript 1 <\s>
<s> when passion's trance is overpast if tenderness and truth could last or live whilst all wild feelings keep some mortal slumber dark and deep i should not weep i should not weep <\s>
<s> it were enough to feel to see thy soft eyes gazing tenderly and dream the rest and burn and be the secret food of fires unseen couldst thou but be as thou hast been 10 3 <\s>
<s> after the slumber of the year the woodland violets reappear all things revive in field or grove and sky and sea but two which move and form all others life and love <\s>

<s> the golden gates of sleep unbar where strength and beauty met together kindle their image like a star in a sea of glassy weather <\s>

<s> let eyes not see their own delight haste swift hour and thy flight 10 oft renew <\s>
<s> fairies sprites and angels keep her <\s>
<s> holy stars permit no wrong <\s>

<s> there is a transcript headed sonnet to the republic of benevento in the harvard manuscript book nor happiness nor majesty nor fame nor peace nor strength nor skill in arms or arts shepherd those herds whom tyranny makes tame verse echoes not one beating of their hearts history is but the shadow of their shame 5 art veils her glass or from the pageant starts as to oblivion their blind millions fleet staining that heaven with obscene imagery of their own likeness <\s>
<s> what are numbers knit by force or custom <\s>
<s> man who man would be 10 must rule the empire of himself in it must be supreme establishing his throne on vanquished will quelling the anarchy of hopes and fears being himself alone <\s>
<s> shelley in the keepsake 1829 1 <\s>
<s> do you not hear the aziola cry <\s>

<s> how elate i felt to know that it was nothing human no mockery of myself to fear or hate and mary saw my soul 10 and laughed and said disquiet yourself not tis nothing but a little downy owl <\s>
<s> many an eventide thy music i had heard by wood and stream meadow and mountain side 15 and fields and marshes wide such as nor voice nor lute nor wind nor bird the soul ever stirred unlike and far sweeter than them all <\s>
<s> from that moment i 20 loved thee and thy sad cry <\s>

<s> there is a transcript headed sonnet to the republic of benevento in the harvard manuscript book nor happiness nor majesty nor fame nor peace nor strength nor skill in arms or arts shepherd those herds whom tyranny makes tame verse echoes not one beating of their hearts history is but the shadow of their shame 5 art veils her glass or from the pageant starts as to oblivion their blind millions fleet staining that heaven with obscene imagery of their own likeness <\s>
<s> what are numbers knit by force or custom <\s>
<s> man who man would be 10 must rule the empire of himself in it must be supreme establishing his throne on vanquished will quelling the anarchy of hopes and fears being himself alone <\s>

<s> there is a transcript headed sonnet to the republic of benevento in the harvard manuscript book nor happiness nor majesty nor fame nor peace nor strength nor skill in arms or arts shepherd those herds whom tyranny makes tame verse echoes not one beating of their hearts history is but the shadow of their shame 5 art veils her glass or from the pageant starts as to oblivion their blind millions fleet staining that heaven with obscene imagery of their own likeness <\s>
<s> what are numbers knit by force or custom <\s>
<s> man who man would be 10 must rule the empire of himself in it must be supreme establishing his throne on vanquished will quelling the anarchy of hopes and fears being himself alone <\s>
<s> shelley in the keepsake 1829 1 <\s>
<s> do you not hear the aziola cry <\s>
<s> methinks she must be nigh said mary as we sate in dusk ere stars were lit or candles brought and i who thought 5 this aziola was some tedious woman asked who is aziola <\s>
<s> how elate i felt to know that it was nothing human no mockery of myself to fear or hate and mary saw my soul 10 and laughed and said disquiet yourself not tis nothing but a little downy owl <\s>
<s> many an eventide thy music i had heard by wood and stream meadow and mountain side 15 and fields and marshes wide such as nor voice nor lute nor wind nor bird the soul ever stirred unlike and far sweeter than them all <\s>
<s> from that moment i 20 loved thee and thy sad cry <\s>

<s> there is a transcript headed sonnet to the republic of benevento in the harvard manuscript book nor happiness nor majesty nor fame nor peace nor strength nor skill in arms or arts shepherd those herds whom tyranny makes tame verse echoes not one beating of their hearts history is but the shadow of their shame 5 art veils her glass or from the pageant starts as to oblivion their blind millions fleet staining that heaven with obscene imagery of their own likeness <\s>
<s> what are numbers knit by force or custom <\s>
<s> man who man would be 10 must rule the empire of himself in it must be supreme establishing his throne on vanquished will quelling the anarchy of hopes and fears being himself alone <\s>

<s> do you not hear the aziola cry <\s>

<s> how elate i felt to know that it was nothing human no mockery of myself to fear or hate and mary saw my soul 10 and laughed and said disquiet yourself not tis nothing but a little downy owl <\s>
<s> many an eventide thy music i had heard by wood and stream meadow and mountain side 15 and fields and marshes wide such as nor voice nor lute nor wind nor bird the soul ever stirred unlike and far sweeter than them all <\s>
<s> from that moment i 20 loved thee and thy sad cry <\s>

<s> how elate i felt to know that it was nothing human no mockery of myself to fear or hate and mary saw my soul 10 and laughed and said disquiet yourself not tis nothing but a little downy owl <\s>

<s> the crane o'er seas and forests seeks her home no bird so wild but has its quiet nest when it no more would roam the sleepless billows on the ocean's breast break like a bursting heart and die in foam 45 and thus at length find rest doubtless there is a place of peace where my weak heart and all its throbs will cease <\s>

<s> one word is too often profaned for me to profane it one feeling too falsely disdained for thee to disdain it one hope is too like despair 5 for prudence to smother and pity from thee more dear than that from another <\s>

<s> after the slumber of the year the woodland violets reappear all things revive in field or grove and sky and sea but two which move and form all others life and love <\s>

<s> published with hellas 1821 what <\s>
<s> alive and so bold o earth <\s>
<s> art thou not overbold <\s>
<s> leapest thou forth as of old in the light of thy morning mirth the last of the flock of the starry fold <\s>
<s> leapest thou forth as of old <\s>
<s> are not the limbs still when the ghost is fled and canst thou move napoleon being dead <\s>
<s> is not thy quick heart cold <\s>
<s> what spark is alive on thy hearth <\s>
<s> is not his death knell knolled <\s>
<s> and livest thou still mother earth <\s>
<s> thou wert warming thy fingers old o'er the embers covered and cold of that most fiery spirit when it fled 15 what mother do you laugh now he is dead <\s>
<s> who has known me of old replied earth or who has my story told <\s>
<s> it is thou who art overbold <\s>
<s> and the lightning of scorn laughed forth 20 as she sung to my bosom i fold all my sons when their knell is knolled and so with living motion all are fed and the quick spring like weeds out of the dead <\s>
<s> still alive and still bold shouted earth 25 i grow bolder and still more bold <\s>
<s> the dead fill me ten thousandfold fuller of speed and splendour and mirth <\s>
<s> i was cloudy and sullen and cold like a frozen chaos uprolled 30 till by the spirit of the mighty dead my heart grew warm <\s>
<s> i feed on whom i fed <\s>
<s> ay alive and still bold <\s>
<s> muttered earth napoleon's fierce spirit rolled in terror and blood and gold 35 a torrent of ruin to death from his birth <\s>
<s> leave the millions who follow to mould the metal before it be cold and weave into his shame which like the dead shrouds me the hopes that from his glory fled <\s>

<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a transcript headed sonnet to the republic of benevento in the harvard manuscript book nor happiness nor majesty nor fame nor peace nor strength nor skill in arms or arts shepherd those herds whom tyranny makes tame verse echoes not one beating of their hearts history is but the shadow of their shame 5 art veils her glass or from the pageant starts as to oblivion their blind millions fleet staining that heaven with obscene imagery of their own likeness <\s>
<s> what are numbers knit by force or custom <\s>
<s> man who man would be 10 must rule the empire of himself in it must be supreme establishing his throne on vanquished will quelling the anarchy of hopes and fears being himself alone <\s>
<s> shelley in the keepsake 1829 1 <\s>
<s> do you not hear the aziola cry <\s>
<s> methinks she must be nigh said mary as we sate in dusk ere stars were lit or candles brought and i who thought 5 this aziola was some tedious woman asked who is aziola <\s>
<s> how elate i felt to know that it was nothing human no mockery of myself to fear or hate and mary saw my soul 10 and laughed and said disquiet yourself not tis nothing but a little downy owl <\s>
<s> many an eventide thy music i had heard by wood and stream meadow and mountain side 15 and fields and marshes wide such as nor voice nor lute nor wind nor bird the soul ever stirred unlike and far sweeter than them all <\s>
<s> from that moment i 20 loved thee and thy sad cry <\s>

<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 1 <\s>
<s> on whose last steps i climb trembling at that where i had stood before when will return the glory of your prime <\s>
<s> no more oh never more <\s>
<s> out of the day and night a joy has taken flight fresh spring and summer and winter hoar move my faint heart with grief but with delight no more oh never more <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 where it is entitled a lament <\s>
<s> three manuscript copies are extant the trelawny manuscript remembrance the harvard manuscript song and the houghton manuscript the last written by shelley on a flyleaf of a copy of adonais 1 <\s>
<s> swifter far than summer's flight swifter far than youth's delight swifter far than happy night art thou come and gone as the earth when leaves are dead 5 as the night when sleep is sped as the heart when joy is fled i am left lone alone <\s>
<s> the swallow summer comes again the owlet night resumes her reign 10 but the wild swan youth is fain to fly with thee false as thou my heart each day desires the morrow sleep itself is turned to sorrow vainly would my winter borrow 15 sunny leaves from any bough <\s>
<s> lilies for a bridal bed roses for a matron's head violets for a maiden dead pansies let my flowers be 20 on the living grave i bear scatter them without a tear let no friend however dear waste one hope one fear for me <\s>

<s> published in ascham's edition of the poems 1834 <\s>
<s> there is a copy amongst the trelawny manuscripts 1 <\s>
<s> the serpent is shut out from paradise <\s>
<s> the wounded deer must seek the herb no more in which its heart cure lies the widowed dove must cease to haunt a bower like that from which its mate with feigned sighs 5 fled in the april hour <\s>
<s> i too must seldom seek again near happy friends a mitigated pain <\s>
<s> of hatred i am proud with scorn content indifference that once hurt me now is grown 10 itself indifferent but not to speak of love pity alone can break a spirit already more than bent <\s>
<s> the miserable one turns the mind's poison into food 15 its medicine is tears its evil good <\s>
<s> therefore if now i see you seldomer dear friends dear friend <\s>
<s> know that i only fly your looks because they stir griefs that should sleep and hopes that cannot die 20 the very comfort that they minister i scarce can bear yet i so deeply is the arrow gone should quickly perish if it were withdrawn <\s>
<s> when i return to my cold home you ask 25 why i am not as i have ever been <\s>
<s> you spoil me for the task of acting a forced part in life's dull scene of wearing on my brow the idle mask of author great or mean 30 in the world's carnival <\s>
<s> i sought peace thus and but in you i found it not <\s>
<s> full half an hour to day i tried my lot with various flowers and every one still said she loves me loves me not <\s>
<s> 35 and if this meant a vision long since fled if it meant fortune fame or peace of thought if it meant but i dread to speak what you may know too well still there was truth in the sad oracle <\s>
<s> the crane o'er seas and forests seeks her home no bird so wild but has its quiet nest when it no more would roam the sleepless billows on the ocean's breast break like a bursting heart and die in foam 45 and thus at length find rest doubtless there is a place of peace where my weak heart and all its throbs will cease <\s>
<s> i asked her yesterday if she believed that i had resolution <\s>
<s> one who had 50 would ne'er have thus relieved his heart with words but what his judgement bade would do and leave the scorner unrelieved <\s>
<s> these verses are too sad to send to you but that i know 55 happy yourself you feel another's woe <\s>

<s> of hatred i am proud with scorn content indifference that once hurt me now is grown 10 itself indifferent but not to speak of love pity alone can break a spirit already more than bent <\s>

<s> therefore if now i see you seldomer dear friends dear friend <\s>
<s> know that i only fly your looks because they stir griefs that should sleep and hopes that cannot die 20 the very comfort that they minister i scarce can bear yet i so deeply is the arrow gone should quickly perish if it were withdrawn <\s>
<s> when i return to my cold home you ask 25 why i am not as i have ever been <\s>
<s> you spoil me for the task of acting a forced part in life's dull scene of wearing on my brow the idle mask of author great or mean 30 in the world's carnival <\s>
<s> i sought peace thus and but in you i found it not <\s>
<s> full half an hour to day i tried my lot with various flowers and every one still said she loves me loves me not <\s>
<s> 35 and if this meant a vision long since fled if it meant fortune fame or peace of thought if it meant but i dread to speak what you may know too well still there was truth in the sad oracle <\s>

<s> there is a transcript headed sonnet to the republic of benevento in the harvard manuscript book nor happiness nor majesty nor fame nor peace nor strength nor skill in arms or arts shepherd those herds whom tyranny makes tame verse echoes not one beating of their hearts history is but the shadow of their shame 5 art veils her glass or from the pageant starts as to oblivion their blind millions fleet staining that heaven with obscene imagery of their own likeness <\s>
<s> what are numbers knit by force or custom <\s>
<s> man who man would be 10 must rule the empire of himself in it must be supreme establishing his throne on vanquished will quelling the anarchy of hopes and fears being himself alone <\s>

<s> do you not hear the aziola cry <\s>
<s> methinks she must be nigh said mary as we sate in dusk ere stars were lit or candles brought and i who thought 5 this aziola was some tedious woman asked who is aziola <\s>
<s> how elate i felt to know that it was nothing human no mockery of myself to fear or hate and mary saw my soul 10 and laughed and said disquiet yourself not tis nothing but a little downy owl <\s>
<s> many an eventide thy music i had heard by wood and stream meadow and mountain side 15 and fields and marshes wide such as nor voice nor lute nor wind nor bird the soul ever stirred unlike and far sweeter than them all <\s>
<s> from that moment i 20 loved thee and thy sad cry <\s>

<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a transcript headed sonnet to the republic of benevento in the harvard manuscript book nor happiness nor majesty nor fame nor peace nor strength nor skill in arms or arts shepherd those herds whom tyranny makes tame verse echoes not one beating of their hearts history is but the shadow of their shame 5 art veils her glass or from the pageant starts as to oblivion their blind millions fleet staining that heaven with obscene imagery of their own likeness <\s>
<s> what are numbers knit by force or custom <\s>
<s> man who man would be 10 must rule the empire of himself in it must be supreme establishing his throne on vanquished will quelling the anarchy of hopes and fears being himself alone <\s>
<s> shelley in the keepsake 1829 1 <\s>
<s> do you not hear the aziola cry <\s>
<s> methinks she must be nigh said mary as we sate in dusk ere stars were lit or candles brought and i who thought 5 this aziola was some tedious woman asked who is aziola <\s>
<s> how elate i felt to know that it was nothing human no mockery of myself to fear or hate and mary saw my soul 10 and laughed and said disquiet yourself not tis nothing but a little downy owl <\s>
<s> many an eventide thy music i had heard by wood and stream meadow and mountain side 15 and fields and marshes wide such as nor voice nor lute nor wind nor bird the soul ever stirred unlike and far sweeter than them all <\s>
<s> from that moment i 20 loved thee and thy sad cry <\s>

<s> the serpent is shut out from paradise <\s>
<s> the wounded deer must seek the herb no more in which its heart cure lies the widowed dove must cease to haunt a bower like that from which its mate with feigned sighs 5 fled in the april hour <\s>
<s> i too must seldom seek again near happy friends a mitigated pain <\s>
<s> of hatred i am proud with scorn content indifference that once hurt me now is grown 10 itself indifferent but not to speak of love pity alone can break a spirit already more than bent <\s>
<s> the miserable one turns the mind's poison into food 15 its medicine is tears its evil good <\s>
<s> therefore if now i see you seldomer dear friends dear friend <\s>
<s> know that i only fly your looks because they stir griefs that should sleep and hopes that cannot die 20 the very comfort that they minister i scarce can bear yet i so deeply is the arrow gone should quickly perish if it were withdrawn <\s>
<s> when i return to my cold home you ask 25 why i am not as i have ever been <\s>
<s> you spoil me for the task of acting a forced part in life's dull scene of wearing on my brow the idle mask of author great or mean 30 in the world's carnival <\s>
<s> i sought peace thus and but in you i found it not <\s>
<s> full half an hour to day i tried my lot with various flowers and every one still said she loves me loves me not <\s>
<s> 35 and if this meant a vision long since fled if it meant fortune fame or peace of thought if it meant but i dread to speak what you may know too well still there was truth in the sad oracle <\s>
<s> the crane o'er seas and forests seeks her home no bird so wild but has its quiet nest when it no more would roam the sleepless billows on the ocean's breast break like a bursting heart and die in foam 45 and thus at length find rest doubtless there is a place of peace where my weak heart and all its throbs will cease <\s>
<s> i asked her yesterday if she believed that i had resolution <\s>
<s> one who had 50 would ne'er have thus relieved his heart with words but what his judgement bade would do and leave the scorner unrelieved <\s>
<s> these verses are too sad to send to you but that i know 55 happy yourself you feel another's woe <\s>

<s> of hatred i am proud with scorn content indifference that once hurt me now is grown 10 itself indifferent but not to speak of love pity alone can break a spirit already more than bent <\s>

<s> therefore if now i see you seldomer dear friends dear friend <\s>
<s> know that i only fly your looks because they stir griefs that should sleep and hopes that cannot die 20 the very comfort that they minister i scarce can bear yet i so deeply is the arrow gone should quickly perish if it were withdrawn <\s>
<s> when i return to my cold home you ask 25 why i am not as i have ever been <\s>
<s> you spoil me for the task of acting a forced part in life's dull scene of wearing on my brow the idle mask of author great or mean 30 in the world's carnival <\s>
<s> i sought peace thus and but in you i found it not <\s>
<s> full half an hour to day i tried my lot with various flowers and every one still said she loves me loves me not <\s>
<s> 35 and if this meant a vision long since fled if it meant fortune fame or peace of thought if it meant but i dread to speak what you may know too well still there was truth in the sad oracle <\s>

<s> there is a transcript headed sonnet to the republic of benevento in the harvard manuscript book nor happiness nor majesty nor fame nor peace nor strength nor skill in arms or arts shepherd those herds whom tyranny makes tame verse echoes not one beating of their hearts history is but the shadow of their shame 5 art veils her glass or from the pageant starts as to oblivion their blind millions fleet staining that heaven with obscene imagery of their own likeness <\s>
<s> what are numbers knit by force or custom <\s>
<s> man who man would be 10 must rule the empire of himself in it must be supreme establishing his throne on vanquished will quelling the anarchy of hopes and fears being himself alone <\s>

<s> do you not hear the aziola cry <\s>
<s> methinks she must be nigh said mary as we sate in dusk ere stars were lit or candles brought and i who thought 5 this aziola was some tedious woman asked who is aziola <\s>
<s> how elate i felt to know that it was nothing human no mockery of myself to fear or hate and mary saw my soul 10 and laughed and said disquiet yourself not tis nothing but a little downy owl <\s>
<s> many an eventide thy music i had heard by wood and stream meadow and mountain side 15 and fields and marshes wide such as nor voice nor lute nor wind nor bird the soul ever stirred unlike and far sweeter than them all <\s>
<s> from that moment i 20 loved thee and thy sad cry <\s>

<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a transcript headed sonnet to the republic of benevento in the harvard manuscript book nor happiness nor majesty nor fame nor peace nor strength nor skill in arms or arts shepherd those herds whom tyranny makes tame verse echoes not one beating of their hearts history is but the shadow of their shame 5 art veils her glass or from the pageant starts as to oblivion their blind millions fleet staining that heaven with obscene imagery of their own likeness <\s>
<s> what are numbers knit by force or custom <\s>
<s> man who man would be 10 must rule the empire of himself in it must be supreme establishing his throne on vanquished will quelling the anarchy of hopes and fears being himself alone <\s>
<s> shelley in the keepsake 1829 1 <\s>
<s> do you not hear the aziola cry <\s>
<s> methinks she must be nigh said mary as we sate in dusk ere stars were lit or candles brought and i who thought 5 this aziola was some tedious woman asked who is aziola <\s>
<s> how elate i felt to know that it was nothing human no mockery of myself to fear or hate and mary saw my soul 10 and laughed and said disquiet yourself not tis nothing but a little downy owl <\s>
<s> many an eventide thy music i had heard by wood and stream meadow and mountain side 15 and fields and marshes wide such as nor voice nor lute nor wind nor bird the soul ever stirred unlike and far sweeter than them all <\s>
<s> from that moment i 20 loved thee and thy sad cry <\s>

<s> the serpent is shut out from paradise <\s>
<s> the wounded deer must seek the herb no more in which its heart cure lies the widowed dove must cease to haunt a bower like that from which its mate with feigned sighs 5 fled in the april hour <\s>
<s> i too must seldom seek again near happy friends a mitigated pain <\s>
<s> of hatred i am proud with scorn content indifference that once hurt me now is grown 10 itself indifferent but not to speak of love pity alone can break a spirit already more than bent <\s>
<s> the miserable one turns the mind's poison into food 15 its medicine is tears its evil good <\s>
<s> therefore if now i see you seldomer dear friends dear friend <\s>
<s> know that i only fly your looks because they stir griefs that should sleep and hopes that cannot die 20 the very comfort that they minister i scarce can bear yet i so deeply is the arrow gone should quickly perish if it were withdrawn <\s>
<s> when i return to my cold home you ask 25 why i am not as i have ever been <\s>
<s> you spoil me for the task of acting a forced part in life's dull scene of wearing on my brow the idle mask of author great or mean 30 in the world's carnival <\s>
<s> i sought peace thus and but in you i found it not <\s>
<s> full half an hour to day i tried my lot with various flowers and every one still said she loves me loves me not <\s>
<s> 35 and if this meant a vision long since fled if it meant fortune fame or peace of thought if it meant but i dread to speak what you may know too well still there was truth in the sad oracle <\s>
<s> the crane o'er seas and forests seeks her home no bird so wild but has its quiet nest when it no more would roam the sleepless billows on the ocean's breast break like a bursting heart and die in foam 45 and thus at length find rest doubtless there is a place of peace where my weak heart and all its throbs will cease <\s>
<s> i asked her yesterday if she believed that i had resolution <\s>
<s> one who had 50 would ne'er have thus relieved his heart with words but what his judgement bade would do and leave the scorner unrelieved <\s>
<s> these verses are too sad to send to you but that i know 55 happy yourself you feel another's woe <\s>

<s> of hatred i am proud with scorn content indifference that once hurt me now is grown 10 itself indifferent but not to speak of love pity alone can break a spirit already more than bent <\s>

<s> therefore if now i see you seldomer dear friends dear friend <\s>
<s> know that i only fly your looks because they stir griefs that should sleep and hopes that cannot die 20 the very comfort that they minister i scarce can bear yet i so deeply is the arrow gone should quickly perish if it were withdrawn <\s>
<s> when i return to my cold home you ask 25 why i am not as i have ever been <\s>
<s> you spoil me for the task of acting a forced part in life's dull scene of wearing on my brow the idle mask of author great or mean 30 in the world's carnival <\s>
<s> i sought peace thus and but in you i found it not <\s>
<s> full half an hour to day i tried my lot with various flowers and every one still said she loves me loves me not <\s>
<s> 35 and if this meant a vision long since fled if it meant fortune fame or peace of thought if it meant but i dread to speak what you may know too well still there was truth in the sad oracle <\s>

<s> there is a transcript headed sonnet to the republic of benevento in the harvard manuscript book nor happiness nor majesty nor fame nor peace nor strength nor skill in arms or arts shepherd those herds whom tyranny makes tame verse echoes not one beating of their hearts history is but the shadow of their shame 5 art veils her glass or from the pageant starts as to oblivion their blind millions fleet staining that heaven with obscene imagery of their own likeness <\s>
<s> what are numbers knit by force or custom <\s>
<s> man who man would be 10 must rule the empire of himself in it must be supreme establishing his throne on vanquished will quelling the anarchy of hopes and fears being himself alone <\s>

<s> do you not hear the aziola cry <\s>
<s> methinks she must be nigh said mary as we sate in dusk ere stars were lit or candles brought and i who thought 5 this aziola was some tedious woman asked who is aziola <\s>
<s> how elate i felt to know that it was nothing human no mockery of myself to fear or hate and mary saw my soul 10 and laughed and said disquiet yourself not tis nothing but a little downy owl <\s>
<s> many an eventide thy music i had heard by wood and stream meadow and mountain side 15 and fields and marshes wide such as nor voice nor lute nor wind nor bird the soul ever stirred unlike and far sweeter than them all <\s>
<s> from that moment i 20 loved thee and thy sad cry <\s>

<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a transcript headed sonnet to the republic of benevento in the harvard manuscript book nor happiness nor majesty nor fame nor peace nor strength nor skill in arms or arts shepherd those herds whom tyranny makes tame verse echoes not one beating of their hearts history is but the shadow of their shame 5 art veils her glass or from the pageant starts as to oblivion their blind millions fleet staining that heaven with obscene imagery of their own likeness <\s>
<s> what are numbers knit by force or custom <\s>
<s> man who man would be 10 must rule the empire of himself in it must be supreme establishing his throne on vanquished will quelling the anarchy of hopes and fears being himself alone <\s>
<s> shelley in the keepsake 1829 1 <\s>
<s> do you not hear the aziola cry <\s>
<s> methinks she must be nigh said mary as we sate in dusk ere stars were lit or candles brought and i who thought 5 this aziola was some tedious woman asked who is aziola <\s>
<s> how elate i felt to know that it was nothing human no mockery of myself to fear or hate and mary saw my soul 10 and laughed and said disquiet yourself not tis nothing but a little downy owl <\s>
<s> many an eventide thy music i had heard by wood and stream meadow and mountain side 15 and fields and marshes wide such as nor voice nor lute nor wind nor bird the soul ever stirred unlike and far sweeter than them all <\s>
<s> from that moment i 20 loved thee and thy sad cry <\s>

<s> the serpent is shut out from paradise <\s>
<s> the wounded deer must seek the herb no more in which its heart cure lies the widowed dove must cease to haunt a bower like that from which its mate with feigned sighs 5 fled in the april hour <\s>
<s> i too must seldom seek again near happy friends a mitigated pain <\s>
<s> of hatred i am proud with scorn content indifference that once hurt me now is grown 10 itself indifferent but not to speak of love pity alone can break a spirit already more than bent <\s>
<s> the miserable one turns the mind's poison into food 15 its medicine is tears its evil good <\s>
<s> therefore if now i see you seldomer dear friends dear friend <\s>
<s> know that i only fly your looks because they stir griefs that should sleep and hopes that cannot die 20 the very comfort that they minister i scarce can bear yet i so deeply is the arrow gone should quickly perish if it were withdrawn <\s>
<s> when i return to my cold home you ask 25 why i am not as i have ever been <\s>
<s> you spoil me for the task of acting a forced part in life's dull scene of wearing on my brow the idle mask of author great or mean 30 in the world's carnival <\s>
<s> i sought peace thus and but in you i found it not <\s>
<s> full half an hour to day i tried my lot with various flowers and every one still said she loves me loves me not <\s>
<s> 35 and if this meant a vision long since fled if it meant fortune fame or peace of thought if it meant but i dread to speak what you may know too well still there was truth in the sad oracle <\s>
<s> the crane o'er seas and forests seeks her home no bird so wild but has its quiet nest when it no more would roam the sleepless billows on the ocean's breast break like a bursting heart and die in foam 45 and thus at length find rest doubtless there is a place of peace where my weak heart and all its throbs will cease <\s>
<s> i asked her yesterday if she believed that i had resolution <\s>
<s> one who had 50 would ne'er have thus relieved his heart with words but what his judgement bade would do and leave the scorner unrelieved <\s>
<s> these verses are too sad to send to you but that i know 55 happy yourself you feel another's woe <\s>

<s> of hatred i am proud with scorn content indifference that once hurt me now is grown 10 itself indifferent but not to speak of love pity alone can break a spirit already more than bent <\s>

<s> therefore if now i see you seldomer dear friends dear friend <\s>
<s> know that i only fly your looks because they stir griefs that should sleep and hopes that cannot die 20 the very comfort that they minister i scarce can bear yet i so deeply is the arrow gone should quickly perish if it were withdrawn <\s>
<s> when i return to my cold home you ask 25 why i am not as i have ever been <\s>
<s> you spoil me for the task of acting a forced part in life's dull scene of wearing on my brow the idle mask of author great or mean 30 in the world's carnival <\s>
<s> i sought peace thus and but in you i found it not <\s>
<s> full half an hour to day i tried my lot with various flowers and every one still said she loves me loves me not <\s>
<s> 35 and if this meant a vision long since fled if it meant fortune fame or peace of thought if it meant but i dread to speak what you may know too well still there was truth in the sad oracle <\s>

<s> there is a transcript headed sonnet to the republic of benevento in the harvard manuscript book nor happiness nor majesty nor fame nor peace nor strength nor skill in arms or arts shepherd those herds whom tyranny makes tame verse echoes not one beating of their hearts history is but the shadow of their shame 5 art veils her glass or from the pageant starts as to oblivion their blind millions fleet staining that heaven with obscene imagery of their own likeness <\s>
<s> what are numbers knit by force or custom <\s>
<s> man who man would be 10 must rule the empire of himself in it must be supreme establishing his throne on vanquished will quelling the anarchy of hopes and fears being himself alone <\s>

<s> do you not hear the aziola cry <\s>
<s> methinks she must be nigh said mary as we sate in dusk ere stars were lit or candles brought and i who thought 5 this aziola was some tedious woman asked who is aziola <\s>
<s> how elate i felt to know that it was nothing human no mockery of myself to fear or hate and mary saw my soul 10 and laughed and said disquiet yourself not tis nothing but a little downy owl <\s>
<s> many an eventide thy music i had heard by wood and stream meadow and mountain side 15 and fields and marshes wide such as nor voice nor lute nor wind nor bird the soul ever stirred unlike and far sweeter than them all <\s>
<s> from that moment i 20 loved thee and thy sad cry <\s>

<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a transcript headed sonnet to the republic of benevento in the harvard manuscript book nor happiness nor majesty nor fame nor peace nor strength nor skill in arms or arts shepherd those herds whom tyranny makes tame verse echoes not one beating of their hearts history is but the shadow of their shame 5 art veils her glass or from the pageant starts as to oblivion their blind millions fleet staining that heaven with obscene imagery of their own likeness <\s>
<s> what are numbers knit by force or custom <\s>
<s> man who man would be 10 must rule the empire of himself in it must be supreme establishing his throne on vanquished will quelling the anarchy of hopes and fears being himself alone <\s>
<s> shelley in the keepsake 1829 1 <\s>
<s> do you not hear the aziola cry <\s>
<s> methinks she must be nigh said mary as we sate in dusk ere stars were lit or candles brought and i who thought 5 this aziola was some tedious woman asked who is aziola <\s>
<s> how elate i felt to know that it was nothing human no mockery of myself to fear or hate and mary saw my soul 10 and laughed and said disquiet yourself not tis nothing but a little downy owl <\s>
<s> many an eventide thy music i had heard by wood and stream meadow and mountain side 15 and fields and marshes wide such as nor voice nor lute nor wind nor bird the soul ever stirred unlike and far sweeter than them all <\s>
<s> from that moment i 20 loved thee and thy sad cry <\s>

<s> the serpent is shut out from paradise <\s>
<s> the wounded deer must seek the herb no more in which its heart cure lies the widowed dove must cease to haunt a bower like that from which its mate with feigned sighs 5 fled in the april hour <\s>
<s> i too must seldom seek again near happy friends a mitigated pain <\s>
<s> of hatred i am proud with scorn content indifference that once hurt me now is grown 10 itself indifferent but not to speak of love pity alone can break a spirit already more than bent <\s>
<s> the miserable one turns the mind's poison into food 15 its medicine is tears its evil good <\s>
<s> therefore if now i see you seldomer dear friends dear friend <\s>
<s> know that i only fly your looks because they stir griefs that should sleep and hopes that cannot die 20 the very comfort that they minister i scarce can bear yet i so deeply is the arrow gone should quickly perish if it were withdrawn <\s>
<s> when i return to my cold home you ask 25 why i am not as i have ever been <\s>
<s> you spoil me for the task of acting a forced part in life's dull scene of wearing on my brow the idle mask of author great or mean 30 in the world's carnival <\s>
<s> i sought peace thus and but in you i found it not <\s>
<s> full half an hour to day i tried my lot with various flowers and every one still said she loves me loves me not <\s>
<s> 35 and if this meant a vision long since fled if it meant fortune fame or peace of thought if it meant but i dread to speak what you may know too well still there was truth in the sad oracle <\s>
<s> the crane o'er seas and forests seeks her home no bird so wild but has its quiet nest when it no more would roam the sleepless billows on the ocean's breast break like a bursting heart and die in foam 45 and thus at length find rest doubtless there is a place of peace where my weak heart and all its throbs will cease <\s>
<s> i asked her yesterday if she believed that i had resolution <\s>
<s> one who had 50 would ne'er have thus relieved his heart with words but what his judgement bade would do and leave the scorner unrelieved <\s>
<s> these verses are too sad to send to you but that i know 55 happy yourself you feel another's woe <\s>

<s> of hatred i am proud with scorn content indifference that once hurt me now is grown 10 itself indifferent but not to speak of love pity alone can break a spirit already more than bent <\s>

<s> therefore if now i see you seldomer dear friends dear friend <\s>
<s> know that i only fly your looks because they stir griefs that should sleep and hopes that cannot die 20 the very comfort that they minister i scarce can bear yet i so deeply is the arrow gone should quickly perish if it were withdrawn <\s>
<s> when i return to my cold home you ask 25 why i am not as i have ever been <\s>
<s> you spoil me for the task of acting a forced part in life's dull scene of wearing on my brow the idle mask of author great or mean 30 in the world's carnival <\s>
<s> i sought peace thus and but in you i found it not <\s>
<s> full half an hour to day i tried my lot with various flowers and every one still said she loves me loves me not <\s>
<s> 35 and if this meant a vision long since fled if it meant fortune fame or peace of thought if it meant but i dread to speak what you may know too well still there was truth in the sad oracle <\s>

<s> there is a transcript headed sonnet to the republic of benevento in the harvard manuscript book nor happiness nor majesty nor fame nor peace nor strength nor skill in arms or arts shepherd those herds whom tyranny makes tame verse echoes not one beating of their hearts history is but the shadow of their shame 5 art veils her glass or from the pageant starts as to oblivion their blind millions fleet staining that heaven with obscene imagery of their own likeness <\s>
<s> what are numbers knit by force or custom <\s>
<s> man who man would be 10 must rule the empire of himself in it must be supreme establishing his throne on vanquished will quelling the anarchy of hopes and fears being himself alone <\s>

<s> do you not hear the aziola cry <\s>
<s> methinks she must be nigh said mary as we sate in dusk ere stars were lit or candles brought and i who thought 5 this aziola was some tedious woman asked who is aziola <\s>
<s> how elate i felt to know that it was nothing human no mockery of myself to fear or hate and mary saw my soul 10 and laughed and said disquiet yourself not tis nothing but a little downy owl <\s>
<s> many an eventide thy music i had heard by wood and stream meadow and mountain side 15 and fields and marshes wide such as nor voice nor lute nor wind nor bird the soul ever stirred unlike and far sweeter than them all <\s>
<s> from that moment i 20 loved thee and thy sad cry <\s>

<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> there is a transcript headed sonnet to the republic of benevento in the harvard manuscript book nor happiness nor majesty nor fame nor peace nor strength nor skill in arms or arts shepherd those herds whom tyranny makes tame verse echoes not one beating of their hearts history is but the shadow of their shame 5 art veils her glass or from the pageant starts as to oblivion their blind millions fleet staining that heaven with obscene imagery of their own likeness <\s>
<s> what are numbers knit by force or custom <\s>
<s> man who man would be 10 must rule the empire of himself in it must be supreme establishing his throne on vanquished will quelling the anarchy of hopes and fears being himself alone <\s>
<s> shelley in the keepsake 1829 1 <\s>
<s> do you not hear the aziola cry <\s>
<s> methinks she must be nigh said mary as we sate in dusk ere stars were lit or candles brought and i who thought 5 this aziola was some tedious woman asked who is aziola <\s>
<s> how elate i felt to know that it was nothing human no mockery of myself to fear or hate and mary saw my soul 10 and laughed and said disquiet yourself not tis nothing but a little downy owl <\s>
<s> many an eventide thy music i had heard by wood and stream meadow and mountain side 15 and fields and marshes wide such as nor voice nor lute nor wind nor bird the soul ever stirred unlike and far sweeter than them all <\s>
<s> from that moment i 20 loved thee and thy sad cry <\s>

<s> the serpent is shut out from paradise <\s>
<s> the wounded deer must seek the herb no more in which its heart cure lies the widowed dove must cease to haunt a bower like that from which its mate with feigned sighs 5 fled in the april hour <\s>
<s> i too must seldom seek again near happy friends a mitigated pain <\s>
<s> of hatred i am proud with scorn content indifference that once hurt me now is grown 10 itself indifferent but not to speak of love pity alone can break a spirit already more than bent <\s>
<s> the miserable one turns the mind's poison into food 15 its medicine is tears its evil good <\s>
<s> therefore if now i see you seldomer dear friends dear friend <\s>
<s> know that i only fly your looks because they stir griefs that should sleep and hopes that cannot die 20 the very comfort that they minister i scarce can bear yet i so deeply is the arrow gone should quickly perish if it were withdrawn <\s>
<s> when i return to my cold home you ask 25 why i am not as i have ever been <\s>
<s> you spoil me for the task of acting a forced part in life's dull scene of wearing on my brow the idle mask of author great or mean 30 in the world's carnival <\s>
<s> i sought peace thus and but in you i found it not <\s>
<s> full half an hour to day i tried my lot with various flowers and every one still said she loves me loves me not <\s>
<s> 35 and if this meant a vision long since fled if it meant fortune fame or peace of thought if it meant but i dread to speak what you may know too well still there was truth in the sad oracle <\s>
<s> the crane o'er seas and forests seeks her home no bird so wild but has its quiet nest when it no more would roam the sleepless billows on the ocean's breast break like a bursting heart and die in foam 45 and thus at length find rest doubtless there is a place of peace where my weak heart and all its throbs will cease <\s>
<s> i asked her yesterday if she believed that i had resolution <\s>
<s> one who had 50 would ne'er have thus relieved his heart with words but what his judgement bade would do and leave the scorner unrelieved <\s>
<s> these verses are too sad to send to you but that i know 55 happy yourself you feel another's woe <\s>

<s> of hatred i am proud with scorn content indifference that once hurt me now is grown 10 itself indifferent but not to speak of love pity alone can break a spirit already more than bent <\s>

<s> therefore if now i see you seldomer dear friends dear friend <\s>
<s> know that i only fly your looks because they stir griefs that should sleep and hopes that cannot die 20 the very comfort that they minister i scarce can bear yet i so deeply is the arrow gone should quickly perish if it were withdrawn <\s>
<s> when i return to my cold home you ask 25 why i am not as i have ever been <\s>
<s> you spoil me for the task of acting a forced part in life's dull scene of wearing on my brow the idle mask of author great or mean 30 in the world's carnival <\s>
<s> i sought peace thus and but in you i found it not <\s>
<s> full half an hour to day i tried my lot with various flowers and every one still said she loves me loves me not <\s>
<s> 35 and if this meant a vision long since fled if it meant fortune fame or peace of thought if it meant but i dread to speak what you may know too well still there was truth in the sad oracle <\s>

<s> there is a transcript headed sonnet to the republic of benevento in the harvard manuscript book nor happiness nor majesty nor fame nor peace nor strength nor skill in arms or arts shepherd those herds whom tyranny makes tame verse echoes not one beating of their hearts history is but the shadow of their shame 5 art veils her glass or from the pageant starts as to oblivion their blind millions fleet staining that heaven with obscene imagery of their own likeness <\s>
<s> what are numbers knit by force or custom <\s>
<s> man who man would be 10 must rule the empire of himself in it must be supreme establishing his throne on vanquished will quelling the anarchy of hopes and fears being himself alone <\s>

<s> do you not hear the aziola cry <\s>
<s> methinks she must be nigh said mary as we sate in dusk ere stars were lit or candles brought and i who thought 5 this aziola was some tedious woman asked who is aziola <\s>
<s> how elate i felt to know that it was nothing human no mockery of myself to fear or hate and mary saw my soul 10 and laughed and said disquiet yourself not tis nothing but a little downy owl <\s>
<s> many an eventide thy music i had heard by wood and stream meadow and mountain side 15 and fields and marshes wide such as nor voice nor lute nor wind nor bird the soul ever stirred unlike and far sweeter than them all <\s>
<s> from that moment i 20 loved thee and thy sad cry <\s>
